  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=5.1)
    The design studio setting provides a suitable backdrop for creative exploration, but lacks specific sensory details that would make it distinctive. The parade creates potential for atmospheric contrast but remains underdeveloped. The timeframe element ("before the first being learns to record its experiences") is awkwardly inserted without meaningful integration into the world-building. The atmosphere relies on telling rather than showing through evocative sensory details.
